Release Version 2025.03.01, March 25, 2025 Submit Arrival Card - Improved the system by adding an optional field for Departure Information in Trip Information section. - Improved the Health Declaration section by making the Upload Certificate field optional. - Improved the user interface by removing the tooltip from the Address field.- Improved the Post Code field to automatically display a default value based on the selected province and district. - Improved Slide Navigation to display only the sections that have been fully completed.- Improved user control by adding a "Delete This Traveler" button for removing individual records. - The List for the [Same as Previous Traveler] option now only shows the entry date into Thailand and the traveler’s name for selection. - Improved interface by renaming the [Next] button to [Preview] and the [Add] button to [Add Other Travelers]. These buttons will be hidden once the maximum number of travelers has been reached. - Improved the Personal Information section by removing the requirement to input the Email Address. - The system has been updated for additional protection in line with OWASP (Open Web Application Security Project) standards. - Improved the Stepper button display by removing the [Previous] button from the Personal Information step and removing the [Continue] button from the Health Declaration step. Update Arrival Card - Improved the system by adding an optional field for Departure Information in Trip Information section. - Improved the Health Declaration section by making the Upload Certificate field optional. - Improved the display of the top message on the Preview page.- Improved the user interface by removing the tooltip from the Address field. - Improved the Post Code field to automatically display a default value based on the selected province and district. - Improved the Personal Information section by removing the requirement to input the Email Address.- The system has been updated for additional protection in line with OWASP (Open Web Application Security Project) standards. - Improved the Personal Information page by removing the 'Previous' button.

Extension of stay is solely at the discretion of the immigration officer. Before the maximum stay of 90 days are eligible to apply for a new type of visa in Thailand. New Visa on Arrival (VoA) Effective Date 15 July 2024 Nationals of the following 31 countries and territories may apply for visa on arrival at the immigration checkpoints on arrival for tourism purpose. Visa Exemption and Visa on Arrival to Thailand Visa Exemption and Visa on Arrival to Thailand วันที่นำเข้าข้อมูล 30 Nov 2023 วันที่ปรับปรุงข้อมูล 25 Jul 2024 | 1,107,526 view Toggle Dropdown New Tourist Visa Exemption Scheme (60 Days) Effective Date 15 July 2024 Nationals of the following 93 countries and territories are entitled to visa exemption for the purpose of tourism business engagements or urgent work or ad-hoc work, for up to 60 days period of stay and can be extended for another period not exceeding 30 days. Extension of stay is solely at the discretion of the immigration officer. Before the maximum stay of 90 days are eligible to apply for a new type of visa in Thailand. New Visa on Arrival (VoA) Effective Date 15 July 2024 Nationals of the following 31 countries and territories may apply for visa on arrival at the immigration checkpoints on arrival for tourism purpose. New Visa on Arrival (PDF)

Visa Exemption and Visa on Arrival to Thailand Visa Exemption and Visa on Arrival to Thailand วันที่นำเข้าข้อมูล 30 Nov 2023 วันที่ปรับปรุงข้อมูล 25 Jul 2024 | 1,107,526 view Toggle Dropdown New Tourist Visa Exemption Scheme (60 Days) Effective Date 15 July 2024 Nationals of the following 93 countries and territories are entitled to visa exemption for the purpose of tourism business engagements or urgent work or ad-hoc work, for up to 60 days period of stay and can be extended for another period not exceeding 30 days. Extension of stay is solely at the discretion of the immigration officer. Before the maximum stay of 90 days are eligible to apply for a new type of visa in Thailand. New Tourist Visa Exemption Scheme (60 Days) Effective Date 15 July 2024 Nationals of the following 93 countries and territories are entitled to visa exemption for the purpose of tourism business engagements or urgent work or ad-hoc work, for up to 60 days period of stay and can be extended for another period not exceeding 30 days. Extension of stay is solely at the discretion of the immigration officer. Before the maximum stay of 90 days are eligible to apply for a new type of visa in Thailand. New Tourist Visa Exemption Scheme (60 Days) Effective Date 15 July 2024

Nationals of the following 93 countries and territories are entitled to visa exemption for the purpose of tourism business engagements or urgent work or ad-hoc work, for up to 60 days period of stay and can be extended for another period not exceeding 30 days. Extension of stay is solely at the discretion of the immigration officer. Before the maximum stay of 90 days are eligible to apply for a new type of visa in Thailand.

Attention : E-Visa applicants are no longer required to submit passports and supporting documents in person at the Royal Thai Embassy/Consulate-General. It is important to note that you are only able to apply if you are currently not in Thailand. After the e-Visa application has been approved, a confirmation e-mail will be sent to applicants, which can be printed out for presenting to airlines and Thai immigration officials when traveling to Thailand. Attention : E-Visa applicants are no longer required to submit passports and supporting documents in person at the Royal Thai Embassy/Consulate-General. It is important to note that you are only able to apply if you are currently not in Thailand. After the e-Visa application has been approved, a confirmation e-mail will be sent to applicants, which can be printed out for presenting to airlines and Thai immigration officials when traveling to Thailand.
